welcome-utility-white\">\n    \t\t     \n<h2 class=\"welcome-utility-white meet__me\">Meet me</h2>\t\t\t<div class=\"textwidget\"><h2 class=\"h1 meet__kevin\">Kevin Rogers</h2>\n\t\t<p class=\"welcome-utility-white\">I spent years traveling the country as a dead-broke stand-up comedian until I discovered how a simple joke formula could be used as a powerful marketing hook and began teaching it to marketers. My strange (but useful) background as a nightclub comic and then as an in-the-trenches salesperson led to the formula which became my Amazon best-selling book <span>The 60-Second Sales Hook.</span></p>\n\t\t<p class=\"welcome-utility-white\">I believe anyone can use the power of their own story to connect better with customers and compel them to take action. They just need to be shown how.</p>\n\t\t<p class=\"welcome-utility-white\">So that’s what I did. I’ve worked closely with high-volume information marketers, corporations and local brick and mortar businesses alike to turn around sluggish ad campaigns. Entrepreneurs and business owners all over the world have used my techniques to skyrocket their profits and grow their businesses at record pace. And now these techniques are available to you inside Copy Chief.</p>\n\t\t<p class=\"welcome-utility-white\">My passion has become connecting talented freelance copywriters to businesses that need them to increase sales, grow businesses, and expose the hidden talents of freelancers.</p>\n</div>\n\t\t          </div>\n\n          <div class=\"col-lg-6\"></div>\n\n        </div>\n    </div>\n
